plane-crazy 2018-12-23 13:49:27 Guys, the purpose of coax rotors is cancel the Torque out right? Then:
Let 100 rpm(s) =one unit of Torque(t)
If we want no Torque,then(t) - (t) =0t
-t=-100 rpm
So the upper rotor should be - 100 rpm
Lower+upper rotor=100rpm-100rpm=0
So........in theory, the upper rotor shouldn't move....right?
plane-crazy 2018-12-23 13:50:34 <@214072411140784128> just let
plane-crazy 2018-12-23 13:53:35 I mean upper+lower=0(cuz there have) Torque
If lower=1,upper should=-1
Upper=1-1=0
Or not?

plane-crazy 2020-08-13 18:22:24 do anyone have the same thought as me, which is there is enough new players for plane crazy after the isolation caused by the outbreak of covid-19 and the egg hunt event? 

i think those new player need some time to develop to a advanced (or better? idk im running out of words) player, i think there are two main negative effects to the game if we dont do so. 

First, it will decrease the game's quality, because this game is a sandbox game, which the game itself only provide a platform for players to create their own creation, in a other word, a large part of the game's content is created by the players, thus, the content/quality of the game and player's skill is positive correlated (for seniors in the game, compare the creations in <#384025409945337856> before and after the egg hunt event). 

Second, it will make PVP mode to a completely meaningless rubbish. According to my observation, new player oftenly use small (low-effort) plane or tutorial creation (especially starter plane with guns and rockets, shredder bug missile or yt guided missile with guns and rockets on it) in PVP, those creation oftenly give them an unfair advantage, making it's hard to use a normal build in PVP mode. You may ask:"then why dont you use the same thing to fight with them?" But, if everyone use the same creation in PVP, then what is the meaning it being one of the mode in a SANDBOX GAME?

In conclusion, i think we shouldn't ask poke to make video about plane crazy initiatively for now.

general 2021-07-22 09:24:33 how to build without brain 101:
1. find a blueprint
2. find the best fit curve equation(s) of it
3. cut the cross surface to many square according to what scale you want
4. differentiate the equation(s) and find the average slope inside every square u cut
5. find a wedge that have a slope closest to your result from (4)
6. place it
7. repeat above steps until you finish all squares
